Card/Describe/Proto_Hydralisks=Launch: Add a Hydralisk Den to your hand.
Card/Describe/Restless_Eggs=Play a random unit card that costs 4 or less resources from your hand. Then draw a card.
Card/Describe/Surging_Larva=Triple the unit count on all of your free Spawn cards. Then play all of your Spawn cards.
Card/Describe/Prey_Spotters=Launch: Add a \"Set an Ambush\" Hive Mind card to your hand.
Card/Describe/Eager_Swarmscout=Launch: Gain 2 Zergling Spawns and 1 Baneling Spawn.
Card/Describe/Monarch_Brood=Each turn the Queens create Creep Tumors. Launch: Add a \"Defend the Hive\" Hive Mind card to your hand.
Card/Describe/Lurker_Cocoons=Morph 2 of your Hydralisks into Lurkers.
Card/Describe/Hive_Queen_Kerrigan=If you've played 3 or more Hive Mind cards, upgrade this. Launch: Shuffle this card into your deck and gain a Defend the Hive.
Card/Describe/Evolving_Swarm=Add Kerrigan's Swarm to your hand. Return an evolution from your discard pile to your hand.
Card/Describe/Overwhelming_Wave=
Card/Describe/Frenzy_Spreader=Launch: Add 2 \"Swarm Them\" Hive Mind cards to your hand.
Card/Describe/Cunning_Scourge=This card has 1 Scourge for each 100 life/shields of enemy air units, to a max of 15 Scourge.
Card/Describe/Baneling_Cocoons=Morph all of your Zerglings into Banelings.
Card/Describe/Brood_Lord_Cocoons=Morph 3 of your Corruptors into Brood Lords.
Card/Describe/Watchful_Predators=The Overseer increases your hand size by 1. Launch: Add a \"Swarm Them\" Hive Mind card to your hand.
Card/Describe/Willful_Roaches=If you have a Hive Mind card selected, this card costs 1 less mineral and gas.
Card/Describe/Willful_Torrasque=When killed, shuffle a Torrasque Revival card into your deck. If you have a Hive Mind card selected, this card costs 3 less mineral and 6 less gas.
Card/Describe/Strange_Larva=Add an Infestor, Defiler, or Brood Queen (chosen randomly) to each of your Spawn cards. Then play all of your Spawn cards.
Card/Describe/Willful_Corruptors=If you have a Hive Mind card selected, this card becomes Heroic.
Card/Describe/Swarm_Queen_Kerrigan=Each turn she adds a Kerrigan's Swarm card to your hand.
Card/Describe/Kerrigan's_Swarm=
Card/Describe/Expendable_Mechs=This card's Viking count equals the number of Marines you've sent via Indoctrination, to a max of 5.
